وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ﴿لَا يَسْتَوِي أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ وَأَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ هُمُ الْفَائِزُونَ﴾ [الْحَشْرِ: ٢٠] ؛ وَذَلِكَ لِأَنَّ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ يَصِيرُونَ إِلَى الدَّرَجَاتِ الْعَالِيَاتِ، وَالْغُرُفَاتِ الْآمِنَاتِ، فَهُمْ فِي مَقَامٍ أَمِينٍ، حَسَنِ الْمَنْظَرِ، طَيِّبِ الْمَقَامِ، ﴿خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا حَسُنَتْ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَمُقَامًا﴾ [الْفَرْقَانِ: ٧٦] ، وَأَهْلُ النَّارِ يَصِيرُونَ إِلَى الدَّرَكَاتِ السَّافِلَاتِ، وَالْحَسَرَاتِ الْمُتَتَابِعَاتِ، وَأَنْوَاعِ الْعَذَابِ وَالْعُقُوبَاتِ، ﴿إِنَّهَا سَاءَتْ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَمُقَامًا﴾ [الْفَرْقَانِ: ٦٦] أَيْ: بِئْسَ الْمَنْزِلُ مَنْظَرًا وَبِئْسَ الْمَقِيلُ مَقَامًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ أَيْ: بِمَا عَمِلُوهُ مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ الْمُتَقَبَّلَةِ، نَالُوا مَا نَالُوا، وَصَارُوا إِلَى مَا صَارُوا إِلَيْهِ ، بِخِلَافِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ فَإِنَّهُ لَيْسَ لَهُمْ عَمَلٌ وَاحِدٌ يَقْتَضِي لَهُمْ دُخُولَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّجَاةَ مِنَ النَّارِ، فَنَبَّه -تَعَالَى -بِحَالِ السُّعَدَاءِ عَلَى حَالِ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا خَيْرَ عِنْدَهُمْ بِالْكُلِّيَّةِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ .

قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّمَا هِيَ ضَحْوَةٌ، فَيَقِيلُ أَوْلِيَاءُ اللَّهِ عَلَى الْأَسِرَّةِ مَعَ الْحَورِ الْعَيْنِ، ويَقيل أَعْدَاءُ اللَّهِ مَعَ الشَّيَاطِينِ مُقْرَّنِينَ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: يَفْرَغُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْحِسَابِ نِصْفَ النَّهَارِ، فَيَقِيلُ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، وَأَهْلُ النَّارِ فِي النَّارِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ .

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: إِنِّي لَأَعْرِفُ السَّاعَةَ الَّتِي يَدْخُلُ فِيهَا أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ، وَأَهْلُ النَّارِ النَّارَ: هِيَ السَّاعَةُ الَّتِي تَكُونُ فِي الدُّنْيَا عِنْدَ ارْتِفَاعِ الضُّحَى الْأَكْبَرِ، إِذَا انْقَلَبَ النَّاسُ إِلَى أَهْلِيهِمْ لِلْقَيْلُولَةِ، فَيَنْصَرِفُ أَهْلُ النَّارِ إِلَى النَّارِ، وَأَمَّا أَهْلُ [الْجَنَّةِ فيُنطلق بِهِمْ إِلَى] الْجَنَّةِ، فَكَانَتْ قَيْلُولَتُهُمْ [فِي الْجَنَّةِ] وَأُطْعِمُوا كَبِدَ حُوتٍ، فَأَشْبَعَهُمْ [ذَلِكَ] كُلَّهُمْ، وَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ .

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ مَيسَرة، عَنِ المِنْهَال، عَنْ أَبِي عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: لَا يَنْتَصِفُ النَّهَارُ حَتَّى يَقِيلَ هَؤُلَاءِ وَهَؤُلَاءِ ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ وَقَرَأَ ﴿ثُمَّ إِنَّ مَرْجِعَهُمْ لإلَى الْجَحِيمِ﴾ [الصافات: ٦٨] .

وَقَالَ العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ قَالَ: قَالُوا فِي الْغُرَفِ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ، وَكَانَ حِسَابُهُمْ أَنْ عُرضوا عَلَى رَبِّهِمْ عَرْضَةً وَاحِدَةً، وَذَلِكَ الْحِسَابُ الْيَسِيرُ، وَهُوَ مِثْلَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَأَمَّا مَنْ أُوتِيَ كِتَابَهُ بِيَمِينِهِ * فَسَوْفَ يُحَاسَبُ حِسَابًا يَسِيرًا * وَيَنْقَلِبُ إِلَى أَهْلِهِ مَسْرُورًا﴾ [الِانْشِقَاقِ: ٧-٩] .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ أَيْ: مَأْوًى وَمَنْزِلًا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وحَدّث صَفْوَانُ بْنُ مُحْرِز أَنَّهُ قَالَ: يُجَاءُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِرَجُلَيْنِ، أَحَدُهُمَا كَانَ مَلِكًا فِي الدُّنْيَا إِلَى الْحُمْرَةِ وَالْبَيَاضِ فَيُحَاسَبُ، فَإِذَا عبدٌ، لَمْ يَعْمَلْ خَيْرًا فَيُؤْمَرُ بِهِ إِلَى النَّارِ. وَالْآخَرُ كَانَ صَاحِبَ كِسَاءٍ فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَيُحَاسَبُ فَيَقُولُ: يَا رَبِّ، مَا أَعْطَيْتَنِي مِنْ شَيْءٍ فَتُحَاسِبُنِي بِهِ. فَيَقُولُ: صَدَقَ عَبْدِي، فَأَرْسِلُوهُ. فَيُؤْمَرُ بِهِ إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ، ثُمَّ يُتْرَكَانِ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ. ثُمَّ يُدْعَى صَاحِبُ النَّارِ، فَإِذَا هُوَ مِثْلَ الحُمَمة السَّوْدَاءِ، فَيُقَالُ لَهُ: كَيْفَ وَجَدْتَ؟ فَيَقُولُ: شَرَّ مَقيل. فَيُقَالُ لَهُ: عُدْ ثُمَّ يُدعَى بِصَاحِبِ الْجَنَّةِ، فَإِذَا هُوَ مِثْلَ الْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ الْبَدْرِ، فَيُقَالُ لَهُ: كَيْفَ وَجَدْتَ؟ فَيَقُولُ: رَبِّ، خَيْرَ مَقيل. فَيُقَالُ لَهُ: عُدْ. رَوَاهَا ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ كُلَّهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يُونُسُ، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَنْبَأَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، أَنَّ سَعِيدًا الصوَّاف حَدَّثَهُ، أَنَّهُ بَلَغَهُ: أَنَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَقْصُرُ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِ حَتَّى يَكُونَ كَمَا بَيْنَ الْعَصْرِ إِلَى غُرُوبِ الشَّمْسِ، وَأَنَّهُمْ لِيَقِيلُونِ فِي رِيَاضِ الْجَنَّةِ حَتَّى يُفْرَغَ مِنَ النَّاسِ، وَذَلِكَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَيْرٌ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَأَحْسَنُ مَقِيلا﴾ .

---

## 25:25-29 — verses 25-29 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs of the terror of the Day of Resurrection and the mighty matters that will occur in it. Among them is the splitting of the sky, its cleaving apart, and its opening up with the clouds, which are canopies of the immense light that dazzles the sight, and the descent of the angels of the heavens on that day, so that they encircle the creatures at the place of the Gathering. Then the Lord, blessed and exalted, comes for the decisive judgment.

Mujahid said: this is as the Almighty said: {Do they wait only for Allah to come to them in canopies of cloud, and the angels, and the matter be decided? And to Allah all matters are returned} [al-Baqarah: 210].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... Ibn Abbas, that he recited this verse: {And the Day the sky is split apart with clouds, and the angels are sent down in successive descent}. Ibn Abbas said: Allah will gather the creation on the Day of Resurrection in one plain, the jinn, mankind, the beasts, the predators, the birds, and all creatures. Then the lowest heaven will split, and its inhabitants will descend, and they are more numerous than the jinn and mankind and all the creatures combined, so they will encircle the jinn, mankind, and all creation. Then the second heaven will split, and its inhabitants will descend, and they are more numerous than the inhabitants of the lowest heaven and than the jinn, mankind, and all creation [so they will encircle the angels who descended before them, and the jinn, mankind, and all creation]. Then the third heaven will split, and its inhabitants will descend, and they are more numerous than the inhabitants of the second heaven and the lowest heaven and than all creation, so they will encircle the angels who descended before them, and the jinn, mankind, and all creation. And so on for each heaven, until the seventh heaven splits, and its inhabitants descend, and they are more numerous than those who descended before them from the inhabitants of the heavens and than the jinn, mankind, and all creation, so they will encircle the angels who descended before them from the inhabitants of the heavens, and the jinn, mankind, and all creation. Then our Lord, mighty and majestic, will descend in canopies of cloud, with the Karubiyyun (the cherubic angels closest to the Throne) around Him, and they are more numerous than the inhabitants of the seven heavens and than mankind, jinn, and all creation. They have horns like the joints of spears, and they are beneath the Throne, having a resounding voice in glorification, declaration of Allah's oneness, and sanctification of Allah, mighty and majestic. Between the sole of one of their feet and his ankle is a distance of five hundred years' journey, and between his ankle and his knee is a distance of five hundred years' journey, and between his knee and his waist-wrap is a distance of five hundred years' journey, and between his waist-wrap and his collarbone is a distance of five hundred years' journey, and between his collarbone and the place of the earring is a distance of five hundred years' journey. And what is above that is a distance of five hundred years' journey, and Hell is at his side. Thus Ibn Abi Hatim narrated it with this wording.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] ... that he heard Ibn Abbas say: When this heaven splits, more angels will descend from it than the jinn and mankind combined, and this is the Day of Meeting, the day when the inhabitants of heaven and the inhabitants of earth meet. The inhabitants of earth will say: has our Lord come? They will say: He has not come, but He is coming. Then the second heaven will split, then heaven after heaven in the same manner of multiplication up to the seventh heaven. More angels will descend from it than all those who descended from the [other] heavens and than the jinn and mankind combined. He said: Then the Karubiyyun angels will descend, then our Lord will come amid the eight bearers of the Throne, between the ankle of each angel and his knee a distance of seventy years' journey, and between his thigh and his shoulder a distance of seventy years' journey. He said: none of these angels looks directly at the face of his companion, and each of them keeps his head lowered between his chest, saying: glory be to the Holy King. And above their heads is something spread out like a cloak, and the Throne is above that.

Then it was held as mawquf (halted report), for its chain revolves around Ali ibn Zayd ibn Jud'an, who is weak, and his narrations generally contain severe strangeness. Something close to this has come in the well-known hadith of the Horn, and Allah knows best.

The Almighty has said: {Then on that Day the Event will occur, and the sky will split, and it will that day be frail, and the angels will be at its edges, and above them on that day eight will bear the Throne of your Lord} [al-Haqqah: 15-17]. Shahr ibn Hawshab said: the bearers of the Throne are eight; four of them say: Glory be to You, O Allah, and praise be to You, praise be to You for Your forbearance after Your knowledge. And four say: Glory be to You, O Allah, and praise be to You, praise be to You for Your pardon after Your power. Ibn Jarir narrated this from him.

Abu Bakr ibn Abdullah said: When the inhabitants of the earth see the Throne descending upon them from above, their eyes will be fixed upon it, their kidneys will tremble within them, and their hearts will fly from their resting places in their chests up to their throats.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] ... Abdullah ibn Amr said: Allah descends, and when He descends there are between Him and His creation seventy thousand veils, among them light and darkness, and the water will make a sound within that darkness, a sound from which hearts are wrenched loose.

This is mawquf, attributed to Abdullah ibn Amr as his own words, and it may perhaps be among the two saddlebags (the two scriptures of the People of the Book he had gathered), and Allah knows best.

The Almighty's saying: {Sovereignty on that day, the true sovereignty, belongs to the Most Merciful, and it will be a difficult day for the disbelievers}, as the Almighty said: {To whom belongs the sovereignty today? To Allah, the One, the Overpowering} [Ghafir: 16]. And in the authentic hadith: "Indeed Allah will roll up the heavens with His right hand, and take hold of the earths with His other hand, then He will say: I am the King, I am the Judge. Where are the kings of the earth? Where are the tyrants? Where are the arrogant ones?"

His saying: {and it will be a difficult day for the disbelievers}, meaning: severe and hard, because it is a day of justice and decisive judgment, as the Almighty said: {So when the trumpet is sounded}, {that, on that day, will be a difficult day, not easy for the disbelievers} [al-Muddaththir: 8-10]. This is the state of the disbelievers on this day. As for the believers, it is as the Almighty said: {The greatest terror will not grieve them, and the angels will receive them, saying: this is your day which you were promised} [al-Anbiya: 103].

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... Abu Sa'id al-Khudri said: it was said: O Messenger of Allah, {a Day whose measure is fifty thousand years}, how long is this day! The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, it will indeed be made light for the believer until it becomes lighter for him than a single obligatory prayer he prays in this world."

His saying: {And the Day the wrongdoer will bite his hands, saying: Oh, would that I had taken a path together with the Messenger}: the Almighty informs of the regret of the wrongdoer who parted from the path of the Messenger and what he brought from Allah of manifest truth, in which there is no doubt, and who took another path apart from the way of the Messenger. When the Day of Resurrection comes, he will regret it at a time when regret will not benefit him, and he will bite his hands in grief and sorrow.

Whether the occasion of its revelation was concerning Uqbah ibn Abi Mu'ayt or another of the wretched ones, it is general, applying to every wrongdoer, as the Almighty said: {The Day their faces are turned about in the Fire, they will say: Oh, would that we had obeyed Allah and obeyed the Messenger! And they will say: Our Lord, we obeyed our chiefs and our great ones, and they led us astray from the path. Our Lord, give them double the punishment and curse them with a great curse} [al-Ahzab: 66-68]. So every wrongdoer will regret to the utmost degree on the Day of Resurrection, and will bite his hands, saying: {Oh, would that I had taken a path together with the Messenger! Oh, woe to me, would that I had not taken so-and-so as a close friend}, meaning: whoever turned him away from guidance and diverted him toward the path of misguidance, among the callers to misguidance, whether that be Umayyah ibn Khalaf, or his brother Ubayy ibn Khalaf, or others.

{He indeed led me astray from the Reminder} [that is, the Qur'an] {after it had come to me}, meaning: after it had reached me. The Almighty said: {And Satan is ever a betrayer of man}, meaning: he abandons him away from the truth, turns him away from it, employs him in falsehood, and calls him to it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ هَول يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَمَا يَكُونُ فِيهِ مِنَ الْأُمُورِ الْعَظِيمَةِ، فَمِنْهَا انْشِقَاقُ السَّمَاءِ وَتَفَطُّرُهَا وَانْفِرَاجُهَا بِالْغَمَامِ، وَهُوَ ظُلَل النُّورِ الْعَظِيمِ الَّذِي يبهر الأبصار، ونزول ملائكة السموات يَوْمَئِذٍ، فَيُحِيطُونَ بِالْخَلَائِقِ فِي مَقَامِ الْمَحْشَرِ. ثُمَّ يَجِيءُ الرَّبُّ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى لِفَصْلِ الْقَضَاءِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: وَهَذَا كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلا أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي ظُلَلٍ مِنَ الْغَمَامِ وَالْمَلائِكَةُ وَقُضِيَ الأمْرُ وَإِلَى اللَّهِ تُرْجَعُ الأمُورُ﴾ [البقرة: ٢١٠] .

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُؤَمِّل، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ يُوسُفَ بْنِ مِهْرَان، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، أَنَّهُ قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَشَقَّقُ السَّمَاءُ بِالْغَمَامِ وَنزلَ الْمَلائِكَةُ تَنزيلا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَجْمَعُ اللَّهُ الْخَلْقَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِي صَعِيدٍ وَاحِدٍ، الْجِنَّ وَالْإِنْسَ وَالْبَهَائِمَ وَالسِّبَاعَ وَالطَّيْرَ وَجَمِيعَ الْخَلْقِ، فَتَنْشَقُّ السَّمَاءُ الدُّنْيَا، فَيَنْزِلُ أَهْلُهَا -وَهُمْ أَكْثَرُ مِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَمِنْ جَمِيعِ الْخَلَائِقِ -فَيُحِيطُونَ بِالْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَبِجَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ. ثُمَّ تَنْشَقُّ السَّمَاءُ الثَّانِيَةُ فَيَنْزِلُ أَهْلُهَا، وَهُمْ أَكْثَرُ مِنْ أَهْلِ السَّمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا وَمِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَمِنْ جَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ [فَيُحِيطُونَ بِالْمَلَائِكَةِ الَّذِينَ نَزَلُوا قَبْلَهُمْ وَالْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَجَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ ] ثُمَّ تَنْشَقُّ السَّمَاءُ الثَّالِثَةُ، فَيَنْزِلُ أَهْلُهَا، وَهُمْ أَكْثَرُ مِنْ أَهْلِ السَّمَاءِ الثَّانِيَةِ وَالسَّمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا وَمِنْ جَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ، فَيُحِيطُونَ بِالْمَلَائِكَةِ الَّذِينَ نَزَلُوا قَبْلَهُمْ، وَبِالْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَبِجَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ. ثُمَّ كَذَلِكَ كُلَّ سَمَاءٍ، حَتَّى تَنْشَقَّ السَّمَاءُ السَّابِعَةُ، فَيَنْزِلُ أَهْلُهَا وَهُمْ أَكْثَرُ مِمَّنْ نَزَلَ قَبْلَهُمْ من أهل السموات وَمِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ، وَمِنْ جَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ، فَيُحِيطُونَ بالملائكة الذين نزلوا قبلهم من أهل السموات، وَبِالْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَجَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ، وَيَنْزِلُ رَبُّنَا عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فِي ظُلَلٍ مِنَ الْغَمَامِ، وَحَوْلَهُ الْكَرُوبِيُّونَ، وهم أكثر من أهل السموات السَّبْعِ وَمِنَ الْإِنْسِ وَالْجِنِّ وَجَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ، لَهُمْ قُرُونٌ كَأَكْعُبِ الْقَنَا، وَهُمْ تَحْتَ الْعَرْشِ، لَهُمْ زَجَل بِالتَّسْبِيحِ وَالتَّهْلِيلِ وَالتَّقْدِيسِ لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، مَا بَيْنَ أَخْمَصِ قَدَمِ أَحَدِهِمْ إِلَى كَعْبِهِ مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَمَا بَيْنَ كَعْبِهِ إِلَى رُكْبَتِهِ مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَمَا بَيْنَ رُكْبَتِهِ إِلَى حُجْزَته مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَمَا بَيْنَ حُجْزَته إِلَى تَرْقُوَتِهِ مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَمَا بَيْنَ تَرْقُوَتِهِ إِلَى مَوْضِعِ القُرط مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ. وَمَا فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَجَهَنَّمُ مُجَنِّبَتُهُ هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ بِهَذَا السِّيَاقِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ، حَدَّثَنِي الْحَجَّاجُ، عَنْ مُبَارَكُ بْنُ فَضَالَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ بْنِ جُدْعَان، عَنْ يُوسُفَ بْنِ مِهْرَان، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ: إِنَّ هَذِهِ السَّمَاءَ إِذَا انْشَقَّتْ نَزَلَ مِنْهَا مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ أَكْثَرُ مِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ، وَهُوَ يَوْمُ التَّلَاقِ، يَوْمَ يَلْتَقِي أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ وَأَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ، فَيَقُولُ أَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ: جَاءَ رَبُّنَا؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: لَمْ يَجِئْ، وَهُوَ آتٍ. ثُمَّ تَنْشَقُّ السَّمَاءُ الثَّانِيَةُ، ثُمَّ سَمَاءٌ سَمَاءٌ عَلَى قَدْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ التَّضْعِيفِ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ السَّابِعَةِ. فَيَنْزِلُ مِنْهَا مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ أَكْثَرُ مِنْ [جَمِيعِ من] نزل من السموات وَمِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ. قَالَ: فَتَنْزِلُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ الكَرُوبيُون، ثُمَّ يَأْتِي رَبُّنَا فِي حَمَلَةِ الْعَرْشِ الثَّمَانِيَةِ، بَيْنَ كَعْبِ كُلِّ مَلِكٍ وَرُكْبَتِهِ مَسِيرَةُ سَبْعِينَ سَنَةً، وَبَيْنَ فَخِذِهِ وَمَنْكِبِهِ مَسِيرَةُ سَبْعِينَ سَنَةً. قَالَ: وَكُلُّ مَلِكٍ مِنْهُمْ لَمْ يَتَأَمَّلْ وَجْهَ صَاحِبِهِ، وَكُلُّ مَلِكٍ مِنْهُمْ وَاضِعٌ رَأْسَهُ بَيْنَ ثدييه يقول: سبحان الملك القدوس. وعلى رؤوسهم شَيْءٌ مَبْسُوطٌ كَأَنَّهُ القَبَاء وَالْعَرْشُ فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ.

ثُمَّ وُقِفَ، فَمَدَارُهُ عَلَى عليِّ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ جُدْعان، وَفِيهِ ضَعْفٌ، وَفِي سِيَاقَاتِهِ غَالِبًا نَكَارَةٌ شَدِيدَةٌ. وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي حَدِيثِ الصُّورِ الْمَشْهُورِ قَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى: ﴿فَيَوْمَئِذٍ وَقَعَتِ الْوَاقِعَةُ وَانْشَقَّتِ السَّمَاءُ فَهِيَ يَوْمَئِذٍ وَاهِيَةٌ وَالْمَلَكُ عَلَى أَرْجَائِهَا وَيَحْمِلُ عَرْشَ رَبِّكَ فَوْقَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ ثَمَانِيَةٌ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١٥ -١٧] قَالَ شَهْرُ بْنُ حَوْشَب: حَمَلَةُ الْعَرْشِ ثَمَانِيَةٌ، أَرْبَعَةٌ مِنْهُمْ يَقُولُونَ: سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ وَبِحَمْدِكَ، لَكَ الْحَمْدُ عَلَى حِلْمِكَ بَعْدَ عِلْمِكَ. وَأَرْبَعَةٌ يَقُولُونَ: سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ وَبِحَمْدِكَ، لَكَ الْحَمْدُ عَلَى عَفْوِكَ بَعْدَ قُدْرَتِكَ، رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ: إِذَا نَظَرَ أَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ إِلَى الْعَرْشِ يَهْبِطُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ، شَخَصَتْ إِلَيْهِ أَبْصَارُهُمْ، ورَجَفت كُلاهم فِي أَجْوَافِهِمْ، وَطَارَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ مِنْ مَقَرّها مِنْ صُدُورِهِمْ إِلَى حَنَاجِرِهِمْ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعْتَمِرُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْجَلِيلِ، عَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: يَهْبِطُ اللَّهُ حِينَ يَهْبِطُ وَبَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ خَلْقِهِ سَبْعُونَ أَلْفَ حِجَابٍ، مِنْهَا النُّورُ وَالظُّلْمَةُ، فيُصَوّت الْمَاءُ فِي تِلْكَ الظُّلْمَةِ صَوْتًا تَنْخَلِعُ مِنْهُ الْقُلُوبُ.

وَهَذَا مَوْقُوفٌ عَلَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو مِنْ كَلَامِهِ، وَلَعَلَّهُ مِنَ الزَّامِلَتَيْنِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿الْمُلْكُ يَوْمَئِذٍ الْحَقُّ لِلرَّحْمَنِ وَكَانَ يَوْمًا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ عَسِيرًا﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِمَنِ الْمُلْكُ الْيَوْمَ لِلَّهِ الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ١٦] وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ: "إن الله يطوي السموات بِيَمِينِهِ، وَيَأْخُذُ الْأَرَضِينَ بِيَدِهِ الْأُخْرَى، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ، أَنَا الدَّيَّانُ، أَيْنَ مُلُوكُ الْأَرْضِ؟ أَيْنَ الْجَبَّارُونَ؟ أَيْنَ الْمُتَكَبِّرُونَ"؟ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَانَ يَوْمًا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ عَسِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: شَدِيدًا صَعْبًا؛ لِأَنَّهُ يَوْمُ عَدْلٍ وَقَضَاءِ فَصْلٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ [فَإِذَا نُقِرَ فِي النَّاقُورِ] ﴾ "، ﴿فَذَلِكَ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَوْمٌ عَسِيرٌ * عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ غَيْرُ يَسِيرٍ﴾ [الْمُدَّثِّرِ: ٨ -١٠] ، فَهَذَا حَالُ الْكَافِرِينَ فِي هَذَا الْيَوْمِ. وَأَمَّا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ فكما قال تعالى: ﴿لا يَحْزُنُهُمُ الْفَزَعُ الأكْبَرُ وَتَتَلَقَّاهُمُ الْمَلائِكَةُ هَذَا يَوْمُكُمُ الَّذِي كُنْتُمْ تُوعَدُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ١٠٣] .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهيعة، حَدَّثَنَا دَرَّاج، عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الخدري قال: قِيلَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ: ﴿يَوْمٍ كَانَ مِقْدَارُهُ خَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ﴾ مَا أَطْوَلَ هَذَا الْيَوْمَ؟ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّهُ لِيُخَفَّفُ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِ حتى يكون أَخَفَّ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ صَلَاةٍ مَكْتُوبَةٍ يُصَلِّيهَا فِي الدُّنْيَا" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَوْمَ يَعَضُّ الظَّالِمُ عَلَى يَدَيْهِ يَقُولُ يَا لَيْتَنِي اتَّخَذْتُ مَعَ الرَّسُولِ سَبِيلا﴾ : يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ نَدَمِ الظَّالِمِ الَّذِي فَارَقَ طَرِيقَ الرَّسُولِ وَمَا جَاءَ بِهِ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ الْمُبِينِ، الَّذِي لَا مرْية فِيهِ، وَسَلَكَ طَرِيقًا أُخْرَى غَيْرَ سَبِيلِ الرَّسُولِ، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ نَدمَ حيثُ لَا يَنْفَعُهُ النَدَمُ، وَعَضَّ عَلَى يَدَيْهِ حَسْرَةً وَأَسَفًا.

وَسَوَاءً كَانَ سَبَبُ نُزُولِهَا فِي عُقْبَةَ بْنِ أَبِي مُعَيط أَوْ غَيْرِهِ مِنَ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ، فَإِنَّهَا عَامَّةٌ فِي كُلِّ ظَالِمٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تُقَلَّبُ وُجُوهُهُمْ فِي النَّارِ يَقُولُونَ يَا لَيْتَنَا أَطَعْنَا اللَّهَ وَأَطَعْنَا الرَّسُولا وَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا إِنَّا أَطَعْنَا سَادَتَنَا وَكُبَرَاءَنَا فَأَضَلُّونَا السَّبِيلا * رَبَّنَا آتِهِمْ ضِعْفَيْنِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالْعَنْهُمْ لَعْنًا كَبِيرًا﴾ [الْأَحْزَابِ:٦٦ -٦٨] فَكُلُّ ظَالِمٍ يَنْدَمُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ غَايَةَ النَّدَمِ، ويَعَض عَلَى يَدَيْهِ قَائِلًا ﴿يَا لَيْتَنِي اتَّخَذْتُ مَعَ الرَّسُولِ سَبِيلا يَا وَيْلَتَى لَيْتَنِي لَمْ أَتَّخِذْ فُلانًا خَلِيلا﴾ يَعْنِي: مَن صَرَفَهُ عَنِ الْهُدَى، وَعَدَلَ بِهِ إِلَى طَرِيقِ الضَّلَالَةِ [مِنْ دُعَاةِ الضَّلَالَةِ] ، وَسَوَاءٌ فِي ذَلِكَ أُمَيَّةُ بْنُ خَلَفٍ، أَوْ أَخُوهُ أُبَيُّ بْنُ خَلَفٍ، أَوْ غَيْرُهُمَا.

﴿لَقَدْ أَضَلَّنِي عَنِ الذِّكْرِ﴾ [وَهُوَ الْقُرْآنُ] ﴿بَعْدَ إِذْ جَاءَنِي﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ بُلُوغِهِ إِلَيَّ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَانَ الشَّيْطَانُ لِلإنْسَانِ خَذُولا﴾ أَيْ: يَخْذُلُهُ عَنِ الْحَقِّ، وَيَصْرِفُهُ عَنْهُ، وَيَسْتَعْمِلُهُ فِي الْبَاطِلِ، وَيَدْعُوهُ إِلَيْهِ.

---

## 25:30-31 — verses 30-31 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about His Messenger and Prophet Muhammad ﷺ always until the Day of Judgment, that he said: {O my Lord, indeed my people have taken this Qur'an as a thing abandoned}. This was because the polytheists would not incline their ears to the Qur'an nor listen to it, as the Exalted said: {And those who disbelieved say: Do not listen to this Qur'an, and speak noisily during its recitation, that perhaps you may overcome} [Fussilat: 26]. Whenever the Qur'an was recited to them, they would raise a great clamor and talk of other things, so that they would not hear it. This is one form of abandoning it. Neglecting its knowledge and its memorization is also a form of abandoning it. Neglecting belief in it and affirming it as true is a form of abandoning it. Neglecting reflection upon it and understanding it is a form of abandoning it. Neglecting to act upon it, to comply with its commands and avoid what it forbids, is a form of abandoning it. And turning away from it toward something else, whether poetry, speech, singing, amusement, talk, or a way of life derived from other than it, is a form of abandoning it. We ask God, the Generous, the Bestower, the One capable of whatever He wills, to free us from whatever angers Him and to employ us in what pleases Him, in the memorization of His Book and its understanding, and in fulfilling its requirements throughout the hours of the night and the ends of the day, in the manner that He loves and is pleased with. He is indeed Generous, Ever-Giving.

Regarding His saying: {And thus have We made for every prophet an enemy from among the criminals}, that is: just as happened to you, O Muhammad, among your people who abandoned the Qur'an, so it was likewise among the nations of old. For God made for every prophet an enemy from among the criminals, who called people to their misguidance and disbelief, as the Exalted said: {And thus have We made for every prophet an enemy, devils among mankind and jinn, inspiring one another with flowery speech in order to deceive. But had your Lord willed, they would not have done it, so leave them and what they invent, that the hearts of those who do not believe in the Hereafter may incline to it, and that they may be pleased with it, and that they may commit what they are committing} [al-An'am: 112-113]. It is for this reason that He said here: {And sufficient is your Lord as a guide and a helper}, that is, for whoever follows His Messenger, believes in His Book, affirms it as true, and follows it. God is his guide and his helper in this world and the next. He said specifically {a guide and a helper} because the polytheists used to turn people away from following the Qur'an, so that no one would be guided by it, and so that their own way would prevail over the way of the Qur'an. It is for this reason that He said: {And thus have We made for every prophet an enemy from among the criminals, and sufficient is your Lord as a guide and a helper}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ رَسُولِهِ وَنَبِيِّهِ مُحَمَّدٍ -صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ دَائِمًا إِلَى يَوْمِ الدين -أنه قال: ﴿يَا رَبِّ إِنَّ قَوْمِي اتَّخَذُوا هَذَا الْقُرْآنَ مَهْجُورًا﴾ ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ الْمُشْرِكِينَ كَانُوا لَا يُصغُون لِلْقُرْآنِ وَلَا يَسْمَعُونَهُ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لَا تَسْمَعُوا لِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ وَالْغَوْا فِيهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَغْلِبُونَ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٢٦] وَكَانُوا إِذَا تُلِيَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْقُرْآنُ أَكْثَرُوا اللَّغَطَ وَالْكَلَامَ فِي غَيْرِهِ، حَتَّى لَا يَسْمَعُوهُ. فَهَذَا مِنْ هُجْرَانِهِ، وَتَرْكُ [عِلْمِهِ وَحِفْظِهِ أَيْضًا مِنْ هُجْرَانِهِ، وَتَرْكُ] الْإِيمَانِ بِهِ وَتَصْدِيقِهِ مِنْ هُجْرَانِهِ، وَتَرْكُ تَدَبُّرِهِ وَتَفْهُّمِهِ مِنْ هُجْرَانِهِ، وَتَرْكُ الْعَمَلِ بِهِ وَامْتِثَالِ أَوَامِرِهِ وَاجْتِنَابِ زَوَاجِرِهِ مِنْ هُجْرَانِهِ، والعدولُ عَنْهُ إِلَى غَيْرِهِ -مَنْ شِعْرٍ أَوْ قَوْلٍ أَوْ غِنَاءٍ أَوْ لَهْوٍ أَوْ كَلَامٍ أَوْ طَرِيقَةٍ مَأْخُوذَةٍ مِنْ غَيْرِهِ -مِنْ هُجْرَانِهِ، فَنَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ الكريمَ المنانَ القادرَ عَلَى مَا يَشَاءُ، أَنْ يُخَلِّصَنَا مِمَّا يُسْخطه، وَيَسْتَعْمِلَنَا فِيمَا يُرْضِيهِ، مِنْ حِفْظِ كِتَابِهِ وَفَهْمِهِ، وَالْقِيَامِ بِمُقْتَضَاهُ آنَاءَ اللَّيْلِ وأطرافَ النَّهَارِ، عَلَى الوجه الذي يُحِبُّهُ وَيَرْضَاهُ، إِنَّهُ كَرِيمٌ وَهَّابٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِيٍّ عَدُوًّا مِنَ الْمُجْرِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا حَصَلَ لَكَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -فِي قَوْمِكَ مِنَ الَّذِينَ هَجَرُوا الْقُرْآنَ، كَذَلِكَ كَانَ فِي الْأُمَمِ الْمَاضِينَ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ جَعَلَ لِكُلِّ نَبِيٍّ عَدُوًّا مِنَ الْمُجْرِمِينَ، يَدْعُونَ النَّاسَ إِلَى ضَلَالِهِمْ وَكُفْرِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِيٍّ عَدُوًّا شَيَاطِينَ الإنْسِ وَالْجِنِّ يُوحِي بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ زُخْرُفَ الْقَوْلِ غُرُورًا وَلَوْ شَاءَ رَبُّكَ مَا فَعَلُوهُ فَذَرْهُمْ وَمَا يَفْتَرُونَ وَلِتَصْغَى إِلَيْهِ أَفْئِدَةُ الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالآخِرَةِ وَلِيَرْضَوْهُ وَلِيَقْتَرِفُوا مَا هُمْ مُقْتَرِفُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١١٢ -١١٣] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَكَفَى بِرَبِّكَ هَادِيًا وَنَصِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: لِمَنِ اتَّبَعَ رَسُولَهُ، وَآمَنَ بِكِتَابِهِ وَصَدَّقَهُ وَاتَّبَعَهُ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ هَادِيهِ وَنَاصِرُهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ. وَإِنَّمَا قَالَ: ﴿هَادِيًا وَنَصِيرًا﴾ لِأَنَّ الْمُشْرِكِينَ كَانُوا يَصُدُّونَ النَّاسَ عَنِ اتِّبَاعِ الْقُرْآنِ، لِئَلَّا يَهْتَدِيَ أَحَدٌ بِهِ، وَلِتَغْلِبَ طَرِيقَتُهُمْ طَرِيقَةَ الْقُرْآنِ؛ فَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِيٍّ عَدُوًّا مِنَ الْمُجْرِمِينَ وَكَفَى بِرَبِّكَ هَادِيًا وَنَصِيرًا﴾ .

---

## 25:32-34 — verses 32-34 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of the abundance of the disbelievers' objections, their obstinacy, and their speech about matters that do not concern them, in that they said: {Why was the Qur'an not sent down to him all at once?} That is: why was this Book, which was revealed to him, not sent down all at once, just as the books before it were sent down, such as the Torah, the Gospel, the Psalms, and other divine books? God answered them regarding that by explaining that it was only sent down in stages over twenty-three years, according to events and occurrences, and according to what was needed of rulings, in order to strengthen the hearts of the believers in it, as He said: {And it is a Qur'an which We have divided, that you may recite it to the people at intervals, and We have sent it down progressively} [al-Isra: 106]. It is for this reason that He said: {That We may strengthen thereby your heart, and We have recited it distinctly, with distinct recitation}. Qatadah said: "And We have explained it with clear explanation." Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: "And We have interpreted it with clear interpretation."

{And they do not come to you with any argument} that is, with any proof or specious claim, {except that We bring you the truth and the best explanation}, meaning: they do not say any statement by which they oppose the truth, except that We answer them with what is true in the reality of the matter, and clearer, more evident, and more eloquent than their statement.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr reported from Ibn Abbas: {And they do not come to you with any argument}, meaning with whatever they seek in order to find fault with the Qur'an and the Messenger, {except that We bring you the truth and the best explanation}, meaning: except that Gabriel would descend from God with the answer to them.

Then in this there is great attentiveness, due to the honor of the Messenger ﷺ, in that revelation would come to him from God with the Qur'an morning and evening, night and day, while traveling and while residing. Each time the angel came to him with the Qur'an it was like the sending down of a book from among the previous scriptures. So this station is higher, more majestic, and greater in standing than that of all his brother prophets, may God's prayers and peace be upon them all. The Qur'an is the most honorable book that God sent down, and Muhammad ﷺ, is the greatest prophet that God sent. God, the Exalted, combined for the Qur'an both attributes together: in the Highest Assembly it was sent down all at once from the Preserved Tablet to the House of Might (Bayt al-Izzah) in the lowest heaven, then after that it was sent down to the earth in stages according to events and occurrences.

Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Nasa'i said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: "The Qur'an was sent down all at once to the lowest heaven on the Night of Decree (Laylat al-Qadr), then after that it came down over twenty years." He said: {And they do not come to you with any argument except that We bring you the truth and the best explanation}, and His saying: {And it is a Qur'an which We have divided, that you may recite it to the people at intervals, and We have sent it down progressively} [al-Isra: 106].

Then the Almighty says, informing of the evil condition of the disbelievers in their return on the Day of Resurrection and their being gathered to Hell in the worst of states and the ugliest of descriptions: {Those who will be gathered to Hell on their faces, those are worse in position and further astray in path}. In the Sahih, from Anas: a man said, "O Messenger of God, how will the disbeliever be gathered upon his face on the Day of Resurrection?" He ﷺ said: "Is not the One who made him walk upon his two feet able to make him walk upon his face on the Day of Resurrection?" And likewise said Mujahid, al-Hasan, Qatadah, and more than one of the exegetes, [and God knows best].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ كَثْرَةِ اعْتِرَاضِ الْكُفَّارِ وَتَعَنُّتِهِمْ، وَكَلَامِهِمْ فِيمَا لَا يَعْنِيهِمْ، حَيْثُ قَالُوا: ﴿لَوْلا نزلَ عَلَيْهِ الْقُرْآنُ جُمْلَةً وَاحِدَةً﴾ أَيْ: هَلَّا أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْهِ هَذَا الْكِتَابُ الَّذِي أُوحِيَ إِلَيْهِ جُمْلَةً وَاحِدَةً، كَمَا نَزَلَتِ الْكُتُبُ قَبْلَهُ، كَالتَّوْرَاةِ وَالْإِنْجِيلِ وَالزَّبُورِ، وَغَيْرِهَا مِنَ الْكُتُبِ الْإِلَهِيَّةِ. فَأَجَابَهُمُ اللَّهُ عَنْ ذَلِكَ بِأَنَّهُ إِنَّمَا أُنْزِلَ مُنَجَّمًا فِي ثَلَاثٍ وَعِشْرِينَ سَنَةً بِحَسَبِ الْوَقَائِعِ وَالْحَوَادِثِ، وَمَا يُحْتَاجُ إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْأَحْكَامِ لِتَثْبِيتِ قُلُوبِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِهِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَقُرْآنًا فَرَقْنَاهُ لِتَقْرَأَهُ عَلَى النَّاسِ عَلَى مُكْثٍ وَنزلْنَاهُ تَنزيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١٠٦] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لِنُثَبِّتَ بِهِ فُؤَادَكَ وَرَتَّلْنَاهُ تَرْتِيلا﴾ . قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وَبَيَّنَّاهُ تَبْيِينًا. وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: وَفَسَّرْنَاهُ تَفْسِيرًا.

﴿وَلا يَأْتُونَكَ بِمَثَلٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِحُجَّةٍ وَشُبْهَةٍ ﴿إِلا جِئْنَاكَ بِالْحَقِّ وَأَحْسَنَ تَفْسِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلَا يَقُولُونَ قَوْلًا يُعَارِضُونَ بِهِ الْحَقَّ، إِلَّا أَجَبْنَاهُمْ بِمَا هُوَ الْحَقُّ فِي نَفْسِ الْأَمْرِ، وَأَبْيَنُ وَأَوْضَحُ وأفصحُ مِنْ مَقَالَتِهِمْ.

قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلا يَأْتُونَكَ بِمَثَلٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِمَا يَلْتَمِسُونَ بِهِ عَيْبَ الْقُرْآنِ وَالرَّسُولِ ﴿إِلا جِئْنَاكَ بِالْحَقِّ وَأَحْسَنَ تَفْسِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: إِلَّا نَزَلَ جِبْرِيلُ مِنَ اللَّهِ بِجَوَابِهِمْ.

ثُمَّ فِي هَذَا اعْتِنَاءٌ كَبِيرٌ؛ لِشَرَفِ الرَّسُولِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ ، حَيْثُ كَانَ يَأْتِيهِ الْوَحْيُ مِنَ اللَّهِ بِالْقُرْآنِ صَبَاحًا وَمَسَاءً، لَيْلًا وَنَهَارًا، سَفَرًا وَحَضَرًا، فَكُلُّ مَرَّةٍ كَانَ يَأْتِيهِ الْمَلَكُ بِالْقُرْآنِ كَإِنْزَالِ كِتَابٍ مِمَّا قَبْلَهُ مِنَ الْكُتُبِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، فَهَذَا الْمَقَامُ أَعْلَى وأجلُّ، وَأَعْظَمُ مَكَانَةً مِنْ سَائِرِ إِخْوَانِهِ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ أَجْمَعِينَ. فَالْقُرْآنُ أشرف كتاب أنزله الله، ومحمد، صلوات اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، أَعْظَمُ نَبِيٍّ أَرْسَلَهُ اللَّهُ وَقَدْ جَمَعَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِلْقُرْآنِ الصِّفَتَيْنِ مَعًا، فَفِي الْمَلَأِ الْأَعْلَى أُنْزِلَ جُمْلَةً مِنَ اللَّوْحِ الْمَحْفُوظِ إِلَى بَيْتِ الْعِزَّةِ فِي سَمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا ثُمَّ نُزِّلَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ مُنَجَّمًا بِحَسَبِ الْوَقَائِعِ وَالْحَوَادِثِ.

قَالَ أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ النَّسَائِيُّ: أَخْبَرَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ، أَخْبَرَنَا دَاوُدَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: أُنْزِلَ الْقُرْآنُ جُمْلَةً إِلَى سَمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا فِي لَيْلَةِ الْقَدْرِ، ثُمَّ نَزَلَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ فِي عِشْرِينَ سَنَةً، قَالَ: ﴿وَلا يَأْتُونَكَ بِمَثَلٍ إِلا جِئْنَاكَ بِالْحَقِّ وَأَحْسَنَ تَفْسِيرًا﴾ ، وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿وَقُرْآنًا فَرَقْنَاهُ لِتَقْرَأَهُ عَلَى النَّاسِ عَلَى مُكْثٍ وَنزلْنَاهُ تَنزيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١٠٦] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ سُوءِ حَالِ الْكُفَّارِ فِي مَعَادِهِمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَحَشْرِهِمْ إِلَى جَهَنَّمَ، فِي أَسْوَأِ الْحَالَاتِ وَأَقْبَحِ الصِّفَاتِ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يُحْشَرُونَ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ إِلَى جَهَنَّمَ أُولَئِكَ شَرٌّ مَكَانًا وَأَضَلُّ سَبِيلا﴾ ، وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ: أَنَّ رَجُلًا قَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ يُحْشَرُ الْكَافِرُ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ؟ فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ الَّذِي أَمْشَاهُ عَلَى رِجْلَيْهِ قَادِرٌ أَنْ يُمشِيَه عَلَى وَجْهِهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ" وَهَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ، [وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] .

---

## 25:35-40 — verses 35-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, threatening whoever denied His Messenger Muhammad ﷺ from among the polytheists of his people and those who opposed him, and warning them of His punishment and painful chastisement, of what He inflicted upon the past nations who denied their messengers. He began by mentioning Musa (peace be upon him), that He sent him and made with him his brother Harun as wazir (minister/supporter), meaning a prophet who would aid, support, and assist him. Pharaoh and his soldiers denied them both, so {God destroyed them, and for the disbelievers are the likes of that} [Muhammad: 10]. Likewise He did with the people of Nuh when they denied His messenger Nuh (peace be upon him). Whoever denies a single messenger has denied all the messengers, since there is no difference between one messenger and another, and even if it were supposed that God sent every messenger to them, they would still have denied him. This is why He said: {and the people of Nuh, when they denied the messengers}, though only Nuh alone was sent to them. He remained among them a thousand years less fifty, calling them to God and warning them of His vengeance, yet only a few believed with him. Therefore God drowned them all, and none of them remained, and no one of the descendants of Adam remained on the face of the earth except the people of the Ark.

{And We made them a sign for mankind}, meaning a lesson from which people take heed, as the Almighty said: {Indeed, when the water overflowed, We carried you in the sailing ship, that We might make it a reminder for you, and that a retaining ear might retain it} [al-Haqqah: 11-12]. That is: We preserved for you, from ships, that which you ride upon in the depths of the seas, so that you might remember God's favor upon you in saving you from drowning, and in making you descendants of those who believed in Him and confirmed His command.

As for His saying, {and 'Ad and Thamud}, the account of their stories has already been discussed in more than one surah, including Surat al-A'raf, in a manner that makes repetition unnecessary.

As for the People of al-Rass, Ibn Jurayj said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: they were the people of a village among the villages of Thamud.

Ibn Jurayj said: Ikrimah said: the People of al-Rass were at Falaj, and they were the People of Yasin. Qatadah said: Falaj was one of the villages of al-Yamamah.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ahmad ibn Amr ibn Abi Asim [al-Nabil] told us, al-Dahhak ibn Makhlad Abu Asim told us, Shabib ibn Bishr told us, Ikrimah told us on the authority of Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying {and the People of al-Rass}, he said: it is a well in Adharbayjan.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, on the authority of Abu Bukayr, from Ikrimah: al-Rass is a well in which they buried their prophet, meaning they interred him there.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, on the authority of Muhammad ibn Ka'b [al-Qurazi], who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The first of the people to enter Paradise on the Day of Resurrection is a black slave, and that is because God, exalted and blessed is He, sent a prophet to the people of a village, and none of its people believed in him except that black slave. Then the people of the village attacked the prophet, dug a well for him, and threw him into it, then sealed it over him with a huge stone." He said: "That slave used to go and gather firewood on his back, then bring his firewood and sell it, and buy with its price food and drink, then bring it to that well, lift that rock, God helping him with it, and lower down to the prophet his food and drink, then put the rock back as it was." He said: "This continued as long as God willed it to continue. Then one day he went to gather firewood as he used to do, and gathered his firewood, bundled it, and finished with it. When he wanted to carry it, he felt drowsy, so he lay down and slept. God struck his ear (made him sleep) for seven years while he slept. Then he awoke and stretched, turned to his other side and lay down again, and God struck his ear for another seven years. Then he awoke and carried his bundle, thinking he had only slept a short while during the day. He came to the village and sold his bundle, then bought food and drink as he used to do. Then he went to the pit, to the place where it had been, and searched for it but did not find it. It had become apparent to his people concerning it, so they had brought the prophet out, and they believed in him and confirmed him." He said: Their prophet used to ask them about that black man: what became of him? And they would say to him: we do not know, until God took the prophet's soul, and the black man awoke from his sleep after that. The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "That black man is indeed the first to enter Paradise."

Ibn Jarir likewise narrated it from Ibn Humayd, from Salamah, from Ibn Ishaq, from Muhammad ibn Ka'b, as a mursal (report with a missing Companion link) report. It contains gharabah (strangeness) and nakarah (objectionable elements), and perhaps it contains idraj (an inserted addition), and God knows best. As for Ibn Jarir, he said: it is not permissible to take these people as being the People of al-Rass who are mentioned in the Qur'an, because God informed concerning them that He destroyed them, whereas these people, it became apparent to them and they believed in their prophet, unless it be that events occurred to them such that they believed in the prophet after the destruction of their forefathers, and God knows best.

Ibn Jarir preferred that what is meant by the People of al-Rass are the People of the Ditch, who are mentioned in Surat al-Buruj, and God knows best.

As for His saying, {and many generations between that}, meaning: many nations, among the multiples of those mentioned, whom We destroyed. This is why He said: {and for each We struck examples}, meaning: We made clear to them the proofs and clarified for them the evidences, as Qatadah said: We removed excuses from them, {and each We shattered utterly}, meaning: We destroyed them completely, as in His saying: {And how many generations have We destroyed after Nuh} [al-Isra: 17].

Al-qarn (generation) refers to a nation of people, as in His saying: {Then We raised up after them other generations} [al-Mu'minun: 31]. Some defined it as one hundred and twenty years. It was also said: one hundred years. It was also said: eighty years. It was also said: forty years. Other views were also given. The most apparent view is that a generation (qarn) is the group of people who are contemporaries in a single era; when they pass away and are succeeded by another generation, that is a second generation, as is established in the two Sahihs from the Messenger of God ﷺ that he said: "The best of generations is my generation, then those who follow them, then those who follow them," the hadith.

As for His saying, {And they have certainly come upon the town that was showered with an evil rain}, meaning the people of Lut, that is Sodom and its associated area, which God destroyed by overturning it and by raining stones of baked clay upon it, as the Almighty said: {And We rained upon them a rain, and evil was the rain of those who were warned} [al-Shu'ara: 173], and He said: {And indeed, you pass by them in the morning, and at night. Do you not then reason?} [al-Saffat: 137-138], and the Almighty said: {And indeed it is on an established road} [al-Hijr: 76], and He said: {And indeed they are both upon a clear road} [al-Hijr: 79]. This is why He said: {Have they then not seen it?}, meaning: so that they would take heed from what befell its people, of punishment and exemplary chastisement, on account of their denial of the messenger and their opposition to God's commands.

As for His saying, {Rather, they did not expect a resurrection}, meaning: those disbelievers who pass by it do not take heed, because they do not expect a resurrection, that is, a return on the Day of Resurrection.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُتَوَعِّدًا مَنْ كَذَّبَ رسولَه مُحَمَّدًا، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، مِنْ مُشْرِكِي قَوْمِهِ وَمَنْ خَالَفَهُ ، وَمُحَذِّرَهُمْ مِنْ عِقَابِهِ وَأَلِيمِ عَذَابِهِ، مِمَّا أَحَلَّهُ بِالْأُمَمِ الْمَاضِيَةِ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ لِرُسُلِهِ، فَبَدَأَ بِذِكْرِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَأَنَّهُ ابْتَعَثَهُ وَجَعَلَ مَعَهُ أَخَاهُ هَارُونَ وَزِيرًا، أَيْ: نَبِيًّا مُوَازرا وَمُؤَيِّدًا وَنَاصِرًا، فَكَذَّبَهُمَا فِرْعَوْنُ وَجُنُودُهُ، فَـ ﴿دَمَّرَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلِلْكَافِرِينَ أَمْثَالُهَا﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ: ١٠] .، وَكَذَلِكَ فعلَ بِقَوْمِ نُوحٍ حِينَ كَذَّبُوا رَسُولَهُ نُوحًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَمَنْ كَذَّبَ بِرَسُولٍ فَقَدْ كَذَّبَ بِجَمِيعِ الرُّسُلِ؛ إِذْ لَا فَرْقَ بَيْنَ رَسُولٍ وَرَسُولٍ، وَلَوْ فُرِضَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ بَعَثَ إِلَيْهِمْ كُلَّ رَسُولٍ فَإِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يُكَذِّبُونَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَقَوْمَ نُوحٍ لَمَّا كَذَّبُوا الرُّسُلَ﴾ ، وَلَمْ يُبْعَثْ إِلَيْهِمْ إِلَّا نُوحٌ فَقَطْ، وَقَدْ لَبِثَ فِيهِمْ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلَّا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا، يَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، وَيُحَذِّرُهُمْ نقَمه، فَمَا آمَنَ مَعَهُ إِلَّا قَلِيلٌ. وَلِهَذَا أَغْرَقَهُمُ الله جَمِيعًا، وَلَمْ يَبق مِنْهُمْ أَحَدٌ، وَلَمْ يَبْقَ عَلَى وَجْهِ الْأَرْضِ مِنْ بَنِي آدَمَ سِوَى أَصْحَابِ السَّفِينَةِ فَقَطْ.

﴿وَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ لِلنَّاسِ آيَةً﴾ أَيْ: عِبْرَةٌ يَعْتَبِرُونَ بِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّا لَمَّا طَغَى الْمَاءُ حَمَلْنَاكُمْ فِي الْجَارِيَةِ * لِنَجْعَلَهَا لَكُمْ تَذْكِرَةً وَتَعِيَهَا أُذُنٌ وَاعِيَةٌ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١١ -١٢] . أَيْ: وَأَبْقَيْنَا لَكُمْ مِنَ السُّفُنِ مَا تَرْكَبُونَ فِي لُجَج الْبِحَارِ، لِتَذْكُرُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ فِي إِنْجَائِكُمْ مِنَ الْغَرَقِ، وجَعْلكم مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ مَن آمَنَ بِهِ وصَدّق أَمْرَهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَعَادًا وَثَمُودَ﴾ قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى قِصَّتَيْهِمَا فِي غَيْرِ مَا سُورَةٍ، مِنْهَا فِي سُورَةِ "الْأَعْرَافِ" بِمَا أَغْنَى عَنِ الْإِعَادَةِ .

وَأَمَّا أَصْحَابُ الرَّسِّ فَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هُمْ أَهْلُ قَرْيَةٍ مِنْ قُرَى ثَمُودَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: أَصْحَابُ الرَسّ بفَلَج وَهُمْ أَصْحَابُ يس. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: فَلَج مِنْ قُرَى الْيَمَامَةِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ أَبِي عَاصِمٍ [النَّبِيلُ] ، حَدَّثَنَا الضَّحَّاكُ بْنُ مَخْلَد أَبُو عَاصِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شَبِيبُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ ، حَدَّثَنَا عِكْرِمَةُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَأَصْحَابَ الرَّسِّ﴾ قَالَ: بِئْرٌ بِأَذَرْبَيْجَانَ.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ عَنْ أَبِي بُكَيْر ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ: الرَّسُّ بِئْرٌ رَسوا فِيهَا نَبِيَّهَمْ. أَيْ: دَفَنُوهُ بِهَا .

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ [الْقُرَظِيِّ] قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ أَوَّلَ النَّاسِ يَدْخُلُ الْجَنَّةَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ الْعَبْدُ الْأَسْوَدُ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ -تَعَالَى وَتَبَارَكَ -بَعَثَ نَبِيًّا إِلَى أَهْلِ قَرْيَةٍ، فَلَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِهِ مِنْ أَهْلِهَا إِلَّا ذَلِكَ الْعَبْدُ الْأَسْوَدُ، ثُمَّ إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْقَرْيَةِ عدَوا عَلَى النَّبِيِّ، فَحَفَرُوا لَهُ بِئْرًا فَأَلْقَوْهُ فِيهَا، ثُمَّ أَطْبَقُوا عَلَيْهِ بِحَجَرٍ ضَخْمٍ قَالَ: "فَكَانَ ذَلِكَ الْعَبْدُ يَذْهَبُ فَيَحْتَطِبُ عَلَى ظَهْرِهِ، ثُمَّ يَأْتِي بِحَطَبِهِ فَيَبِيعُهُ، وَيَشْتَرِي بِهِ طَعَامًا وَشَرَابًا، ثُمَّ يَأْتِي بِهِ إِلَى تِلْكَ الْبِئْرِ، فَيَرْفَعُ تِلْكَ الصَّخْرَةَ، وَيُعِينُهُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهَا، فَيُدْلِي إِلَيْهِ طَعَامَهُ وَشَرَابَهُ، ثُمَّ يَرُدُّهَا كَمَا كَانَتْ". قَالَ: "فَكَانَ ذَلِكَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَكُونَ، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُ ذَهَبَ يوماً يَحْتَطِبُ كَمَا كَانَ يَصْنَعُ، فَجَمَعَ حَطَبَهُ وحَزم وَفَرَغَ مِنْهَا فَلَمَّا أَرَادَ أَنْ يَحْتَمِلَهَا وَجَدَ سِنَةً، فَاضْطَجَعَ فَنَامَ، فَضَرَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَى أُذُنِهِ سَبْعَ سِنِينَ نَائِمًا، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُ هَبّ فَتَمَطَّى، فَتَحَوَّلَ لِشِقِّهِ الْآخَرِ فَاضْطَجَعَ، فَضَرَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَى أُذُنِهِ سَبْعَ سِنِينَ أُخْرَى، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُ هَبَّ وَاحْتَمَلَ حُزْمَته وَلَا يحسبُ إِلَّا أَنَّهُ نَامَ سَاعَةً مِنْ نَهَارٍ فَجَاءَ إِلَى الْقَرْيَةِ فَبَاعَ حُزْمَتَهُ، ثُمَّ اشْتَرَى طَعَامًا وَشَرَابًا كَمَا كَانَ يَصْنَعُ. ثُمَّ ذَهَبَ إِلَى الْحُفَيْرَةِ فِي مَوْضِعِهَا الَّذِي كَانَتْ فِيهِ، فَالْتَمَسَهُ فَلَمْ يَجِدْهُ. وَكَانَ قَدْ بَدَا لِقَوْمِهِ فِيهِ بَداء، فَاسْتَخْرَجُوهُ وَآمَنُوا بِهِ وصدقوه". قال: فَكَانَ نَبِيُّهُمْ يَسْأَلُهُمْ عَنْ ذَلِكَ الْأَسْوَدِ: مَا فَعَلَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ لَهُ: لَا نَدْرِي. حَتَّى قَبَضَ اللَّهُ النَّبِيَّ، وَأهبّ الأسودَ مِنْ نَوْمَتِهِ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ". فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ ذَلِكَ الأسودَ لأولُ مَنْ يَدْخُلِ الْجَنَّةَ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنْ سَلَمَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ مُرْسَلًا. وَفِيهِ غَرَابَةٌ ونَكارَةٌ، وَلَعَلَّ فِيهِ إدْرَاجاً، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَأَمَّا ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فَقَالَ: لَا يَجُوزُ أَنْ يُحْمَلَ هَؤُلَاءِ عَلَى أَنَّهُمْ أَصْحَابُ الرَّسِّ الَّذِينَ ذُكِرُوا فِي الْقُرْآنِ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ أَنَّهُ أَهْلَكَهُمْ، وَهَؤُلَاءِ قَدْ بَدَا لَهُمْ فَآمَنُوا بِنَبِيِّهِمْ، اللَّهُمَّ إِلَّا أَنْ يَكُونَ حَدَثَ لَهُمْ أَحْدَاثٌ، آمَنُوا بِالنَّبِيِّ بَعْدَ هَلَاكِ آبَائِهِمْ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِأَصْحَابِ الرَّسِّ هُمْ أَصْحَابُ الْأُخْدُودِ، الَّذِينَ ذُكِرُوا فِي سُورَةِ الْبُرُوجِ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقُرُونًا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ كَثِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: وَأُمَمًا بَيْنَ أَضْعَافِ مَنْ ذُكر أَهْلَكْنَاهُمْ كَثِيرَةً؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَكُلا ضَرَبْنَا لَهُ الأمْثَالَ﴾ أَيْ: بَيَّنَّا لَهُمُ الْحُجَجَ، ووضَّحنا لَهُمُ الْأَدِلَّةَ -كَمَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أَزَحْنَا عَنْهُمُ الْأَعْذَارَ - ﴿وَكُلا تَبَّرْنَا تَتْبِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: أَهْلَكْنَا إِهْلَاكًا، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَكَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنَ الْقُرُونِ مِنْ بَعْدِ نُوحٍ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١٧] .

وَالْقَرْنُ: هُوَ الْأُمَّةُ مِنَ النَّاسِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿ثُمَّ أَنْشَأْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ قُرُونًا آخَرِينَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ٣١] وحدَّه بَعْضُهُمْ بِمِائَةٍ وَعِشْرِينَ سَنَةً. وَقِيلَ: بِمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ. وَقِيلَ: بِثَمَانِينَ سَنَةً. وَقِيلَ: أَرْبَعِينَ. وَقِيلَ غَيْرُ ذَلِكَ. وَالْأَظْهَرُ: أَنَّ الْقَرْنَ هُمُ الْأُمَّةُ الْمُتَعَاصِرُونَ فِي الزَّمَنِ الْوَاحِدِ؛ فَإِذَا ذَهَبُوا وَخَلَفَهُمْ جِيلٌ آخَرُ فَهُمْ قَرْنٌ ثَانٍ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "خَيْرُ الْقُرُونِ قَرْنِي، ثُمَّ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ، ثُمَّ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ" الْحَدِيثَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أَتَوْا عَلَى الْقَرْيَةِ الَّتِي أُمْطِرَتْ مَطَرَ السَّوْءِ﴾ يَعْنِي: قَوْمَ لُوطٍ، وَهِيَ سَدُومُ وَمُعَامَلَتُهَا الَّتِي أَهْلَكَهَا اللَّهُ بِالْقَلْبِ، وَبِالْمَطَرِ الْحِجَارَةِ مِنْ سِجِّيلٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَمْطَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ مَطَرًا فَسَاءَ مَطَرُ الْمُنْذَرِينَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ١٧٣] وَقَالَ ﴿وَإِنَّكُمْ لَتَمُرُّونَ عَلَيْهِمْ مُصْبِحِينَ * وَبِاللَّيْلِ أَفَلا تَعْقِلُونَ﴾ [الصافات: ١٣٧ -١٣٨] وقال تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنَّهَا لَبِسَبِيلٍ مُقِيمٍ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ:٧٦] وَقَالَ ﴿وَإِنَّهُمَا لَبِإِمَامٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ: ٧٩] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَفَلَمْ يَكُونُوا يَرَوْنَهَا﴾ أَيْ: فَيَعْتَبِرُوا بِمَا حَلّ بِأَهْلِهَا مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ بِسَبَبِ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ بِالرَّسُولِ وَمُخَالَفَتِهِمْ أَوَامِرَ اللَّهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ كَانُوا لَا يَرْجُونَ نُشُورًا﴾ يَعْنِي: الْمَارِّينَ بِهَا مِنَ الْكُفَّارِ لَا يَعْتَبِرُونَ لِأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَرْجُونَ نُشُورًا، أَيْ: مَعَادًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

---

## 25:41-44 — verses 41-44 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, informs of the mockery of the polytheists toward the Messenger ﷺ, whenever they saw him, just as He said: {And when those who disbelieve see you, they take you not except in mockery, [saying], "Is this the one who mentions your gods?"} [al-Anbiya: 36], meaning him with fault-finding and disparagement. And He said here: {And when they see you, they take you not except in mockery, [saying], "Is this the one whom Allah has sent as a messenger?"}, that is, by way of belittlement and contempt, may Allah disfigure them, just as He said: {And already were messengers ridiculed before you, but I gave time to those who disbelieved; then I seized them, and how [terrible] was My penalty} [al-Ra'd: 32].

As for their statement: {He almost would have misled us from our gods had we not been steadfast in [worship of] them}, they mean that he nearly turned them away from the worship of their idols, had they not been patient, held firm, and persisted in worshiping them. Allah, exalted is He, said, threatening and warning them: {But they are going to know, when they see the punishment, who is farthest astray in [his] way}.

Then Allah, exalted is He, said to His Prophet, alerting him that whoever Allah has decreed wretchedness and misguidance for, no one can guide him except Allah:

{Have you seen the one who takes as his god his own desire?} That is, whatever he deems good and regards as pleasing according to the whim of his own soul becomes his religion and his creed, just as Allah, exalted is He, said: {Then is one whose evil deed has been made attractive to him so he sees it as good [like one rightly guided]? For indeed, Allah sends astray whom He wills and guides whom He wills. So do not let yourself perish over them in regret} [Fatir: 8]. For this reason He said here: {Then would you be responsible for him?} Ibn Abbas said: In the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic era) a man would worship a white stone for a period of time, and if he saw another one more beautiful than it, he would worship the second and abandon the first.

Then He said: {Or do you think that most of them hear or reason? They are not except like livestock, rather, they are more astray in [their] way}, meaning: worse off than grazing livestock. For those animals comprehend that for which they were created, whereas these people were created to worship Allah alone, without partner, yet they worship other than Him and associate partners with Him, despite the establishment of the proof against them and the sending of messengers to them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ اسْتِهْزَاءِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ بِالرَّسُولِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، إِذَا رَأَوْهُ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا رَآكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِنْ يَتَّخِذُونَكَ إِلا هُزُوًا أَهَذَا الَّذِي يَذْكُرُ آلِهَتَكُمْ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٣٦] يَعْنُونَهُ بِالْعَيْبِ وَالنَّقْصِ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَإِذَا رَأَوْكَ إِنْ يَتَّخِذُونَكَ إِلا هُزُوًا أَهَذَا الَّذِي بَعَثَ اللَّهُ رَسُولا﴾ ؟ أَيْ: عَلَى سَبِيلِ التَّنَقُّصِ وَالِازْدِرَاءِ -قبَّحهم اللَّهُ -كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدِ اسْتُهْزِئَ بِرُسُلٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فَأَمْلَيْتُ لِلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا ثُمَّ أَخَذْتُهُمْ فَكَيْفَ كَانَ عِقَابِ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٣٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُمْ : ﴿إِنْ كَادَ لَيُضِلُّنَا عَنْ آلِهَتِنَا لَوْلا أَنْ صَبَرْنَا عَلَيْهَا﴾ يَعْنُونَ: أَنَّهُ كَادَ يَثْنِيهِمْ عَنْ عِبَادَةِ أَصْنَامِهِمْ، لَوْلَا أَنْ صَبَرُوا وَتَجَلَّدُوا وَاسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَى عِبَادَتِهَا. قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مُتَوَعِّدًا لَهُمْ وَمُتَهَدِّدًا: ﴿وَسَوْفَ يَعْلَمُونَ حِينَ يَرَوْنَ الْعَذَابَ مَنْ أَضَلُّ سَبِيلا﴾ .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ، مُنَبِّهًا لَهُ أَنَّ مَنْ كَتَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ الشَّقَاوَةَ وَالضَّلَالَ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَهْدِيهِ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا اللَّهُ.

﴿أَرَأَيْتَ مَنِ اتَّخَذَ إِلَهَهُ هَوَاهُ﴾ أَيْ: مَهْمَا اسْتَحْسَنَ مِنْ شَيْءٍ وَرَآهُ حَسَنًا فِي هَوَى نَفْسِهِ، كَانَ دينَه ومذهبَه، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَفَمَنْ زُيِّنَ لَهُ سُوءُ عَمَلِهِ فَرَآهُ حَسَنًا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يُضِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ فَلا تَذْهَبْ نَفْسُكَ عَلَيْهِمْ حَسَرَاتٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ:٨] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿أَفَأَنْتَ تَكُونُ عَلَيْهِ وَكِيلا﴾ . قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ الرَّجُلُ فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ يَعْبُدُ الْحَجَرَ الْأَبْيَضَ زَمَانًا، فَإِذَا رَأَى غَيْرَهُ أَحْسَنَ مِنْهُ عَبَدَ الثَّانِي وَتَرَكَ الْأَوَّلَ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿أَمْ تَحْسَبُ أَنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ يَسْمَعُونَ أَوْ يَعْقِلُونَ إِنْ هُمْ إِلا كَالأنْعَامِ بَلْ هُمْ أَضَلُّ سَبِيلا﴾ أَيْ: أَسْوَأُ حَالًا مِنَ الْأَنْعَامِ السَّارِحَةِ، فَإِنَّ تِلْكَ تَعْقِلُ مَا خُلِقَتْ لَهُ، وَهَؤُلَاءِ خُلِقُوا لِعِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَهُمْ يَعْبُدُونَ غَيْرَهُ وَيُشْرِكُونَ بِهِ، مَعَ قِيَامِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَإِرْسَالِ الرُّسُلِ إِلَيْهِمْ.

---

## 25:45-47 — verses 45-47 (shared commentary)

### Translation

It is from here that Allah, exalted is He, began to set forth the proofs pointing to His existence and His complete power over the creation of varied and opposite things, saying: {Have you not seen your Lord, how He extends the shadow?} Ibn Abbas, Ibn Umar, Abu al-Aliyah, Abu Malik, Masruq, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, al-Dahhak, al-Hasan al-Basri, Qatadah, al-Suddi, and others said: it is what is between the rising of dawn and the rising of the sun. {And if He willed, He would have made it still}, that is, permanent, never disappearing, just as He, exalted is He, said: {Say, have you considered: if Allah made the night perpetual over you until the Day of Resurrection...}, {Say, have you considered: if Allah made the day perpetual over you until the Day of Resurrection...} [al-Qasas: 71-72].

His saying: {Then We made the sun a guide to it} means: were it not that the sun rises upon it, it would not be known, for the opposite is not known except by its opposite.

Qatadah and al-Suddi said: a guide that follows it and comes after it until it takes it over entirely.

His saying: {Then We withdraw it to Ourselves with an easy withdrawal}, meaning the shadow, though it has also been said to mean the sun. {Easy} means gentle. Ibn Abbas said: swift. Mujahid said: imperceptible. Al-Suddi said: an imperceptible withdrawal, such that no shadow remains on the earth except beneath a roof or beneath a tree, the sun having by then overshadowed what is above it.

Ayyub ibn Musa said: {Then We withdraw it to Ourselves with an easy withdrawal} means little by little.

His saying: {And it is He who made the night a garment for you}, meaning it clothes existence and covers it, just as He said: [{By the night when it covers} [al-Layl: 1], and He said] {By the night when it covers her} [al-Shams: 4].

{And sleep a rest}, meaning a cessation of movement for the repose of bodies, for the limbs and organs grow weary from the abundance of movement in the spreading about of the day in pursuit of livelihoods. So when night comes and stillness settles, the movements cease and find rest, and sleep occurs, in which there is repose for the body and the spirit together.

{And made the day a time of spreading out}, meaning people spread out during it for their livelihoods, their earnings, and their affairs, just as He, exalted is He, said: {And out of His mercy He made for you the night and the day, that you may rest therein and that you may seek of His bounty, and that you may be grateful} [al-Qasas: 73].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

مِنْ هَاهُنَا شَرَعَ تَعَالَى فِي بَيَانِ الْأَدِلَّةِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى وُجُودِهِ، وَقُدْرَتِهِ التَّامَّةِ عَلَى خَلْقِ الْأَشْيَاءِ الْمُخْتَلِفَةِ وَالْمُتَضَادَّةِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى رَبِّكَ كَيْفَ مَدَّ الظِّلَّ﴾ ؟ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وابن عمر، وأبو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَأَبُو مَالِكٍ، وَمَسْرُوقٌ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِي، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ: هُوَ مَا بَيْنَ طُلُوعِ الْفَجْرِ إِلَى طُلُوعِ الشَّمْسِ. ﴿وَلَوْ شَاءَ لَجَعَلَهُ سَاكِنًا﴾ أَيْ: دَائِمًا لَا يَزُولُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ أَرَأَيْتُمْ إِنْ جَعَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكُمُ اللَّيْلَ سَرْمَدًا إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ﴾ ، ﴿قُلْ أَرَأَيْتُمْ إِنْ جَعَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكُمُ النَّهَارَ سَرْمَدًا إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٧١ -٧٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ جَعَلْنَا الشَّمْسَ عَلَيْهِ دَلِيلا﴾ أَيْ: لَوْلَا أَنَّ الشَّمْسَ تَطْلُعُ عَلَيْهِ، لَمَا عُرِفَ، فَإِنَّ الضِّدَّ لَا يُعْرَفُ إِلَّا بِضِدِّهِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: دَلِيلًا يَتْلُوهُ وَيَتْبَعُهُ حَتَّى يَأْتِيَ عَلَيْهِ كُلِّهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ قَبَضْنَاهُ إِلَيْنَا قَبْضًا يَسِيرًا﴾ أَيِ: الظِّلَّ، وَقِيلَ: الشَّمْسَ. ﴿يَسِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: سَهْلًا. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: سَرِيعًا. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: خَفِيًّا. وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ؛ قَبْضًا خفَياً، حَتَّى لَا يَبْقَى فِي الْأَرْضِ ظِلٌّ إِلَّا تَحْتَ سَقْفٍ أَوْ تَحْتَ شَجَرَةٍ، وَقَدْ أَظَلَّتِ الشَّمْسُ مَا فَوْقَهُ.

وَقَالَ أَيُّوبُ بْنُ مُوسَى: ﴿ثُمَّ قَبَضْنَاهُ إِلَيْنَا قَبْضًا يَسِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: قَلِيلًا قَلِيلًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمُ اللَّيْلَ لِبَاسًا﴾ أَيْ: يَلْبَسُ الْوُجُودَ ويُغَشيه ، كَمَا قَالَ: [ ﴿وَاللَّيْلِ إِذَا يَغْشَى﴾ [اللَّيْلِ: ١] وَقَالَ] ﴿وَاللَّيْلِ إِذَا يَغْشَاهَا﴾ [الشَّمْسِ: ٤] .

﴿وَالنَّوْمَ سُبَاتًا﴾ أَيْ: قَطْعَا لِلْحَرَكَةِ لِرَاحَةِ الْأَبْدَانِ، فَإِنَّ الْأَعْضَاءَ وَالْجَوَارِحَ تَكِلُّ مِنْ كَثْرَةِ الْحَرَكَةِ فِي الِانْتِشَارِ بِالنَّهَارِ فِي الْمَعَايِشِ، فَإِذَا جَاءَ اللَّيْلُ وَسَكَنَ سَكَنَتِ الْحَرَكَاتُ، فَاسْتَرَاحَتْ فَحَصَلَ النَّوْمُ الَّذِي فِيهِ رَاحَةُ الْبَدَنِ وَالرُّوحِ مَعًا.

﴿وَجَعَلَ النَّهَارَ نُشُورًا﴾ أَيْ: يَنْتَشِرُ الناسُ فِيهِ لِمَعَايِشِهِمْ وَمَكَاسِبِهِمْ وَأَسْبَابِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمِنْ رَحْمَتِهِ جَعَلَ لَكُمُ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ لِتَسْكُنُوا فِيهِ وَلِتَبْتَغُوا مِنْ فَضْلِهِ وَلَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٧٣] .

---

## 25:48-50 — verses 48-50 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This too is an aspect of His complete power and mighty dominion: that He, exalted is He, sends the winds as bearers of glad tidings, meaning of the coming of the clouds after them. The winds are of various kinds, possessing many characteristics in their being made to serve their function. Some of them stir up the clouds, some carry them, some drive them along, some go ahead of the clouds bearing good tidings, some come before all that and sweep the earth clean, and some fertilize the clouds so that they may rain. For this reason He said: {And We sent down from the sky water that is Tahur (pure/purifying)}, meaning: an instrument by which purification is achieved, like sahur (pre-dawn meal, from the same root pattern) and waqud (fuel) and what follows the same pattern. This is the most correct thing said about it. As for those who say that it is a fa'ul form with the meaning of fa'il (active participle), or that it is constructed for intensification or for transitivity, each of these views carries difficulties from the standpoint of language and of legal ruling. This is not the place to elaborate on them. And Allah knows best.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Thabit al-Bunani said: I entered with Abu al-'Aliyah on a rainy day, and the roads of Basra were filthy, and he prayed. I asked him about it, and he said: {And We sent down from the sky water that is Tahur}. He said: the water of the sky purified it.

He also said: [chain] Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab, concerning this verse, {And We sent down from the sky water that is Tahur}: [he said: Allah sent it down as pure water] which nothing renders impure.

And from Abu Sa'id, who said: It was said, "O Messenger of Allah, shall we perform ablution from the well of Buda'ah?" This being a well into which foul matter and the flesh of dogs were thrown. He said: "Water is Tahur; nothing renders it impure." Reported by al-Shafi'i, and Ahmad who deemed it sound, and Abu Dawud, and al-Tirmidhi who deemed it hasan (good), and al-Nasa'i.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Khalid ibn Yazid said: He was with 'Abd al-Malik ibn Marwan, and they mentioned water, and Khalid ibn Yazid said: some of it is from the sky, and some of it is what the clouds draw up from the sea, which is then made fresh by the thunder and lightning. As for what comes from the sea, it produces no vegetation; vegetation comes only from what is from the sky.

It is related from 'Ikrimah that he said: Allah never sends down a drop from the sky except that He causes by it either a plant to grow on the earth or a pearl to grow in the sea. Another said: on land, wheat; in the sea, pearls.

His saying: {That We may give life thereby to a dead land}, meaning: a land whose waiting for rain has been long, being barren, with no vegetation or anything else in it. Then when the rain-bringing life comes to it, it lives, and its hills become clothed with various kinds of blossoms and colors, as He, exalted is He, said: {So when We send down water upon it, it quivers and swells and produces of every joyous kind} [al-Hajj: 5].

{And We give drink thereby to many cattle and men that We have created}, meaning: and that the living creatures, of cattle and of men, may drink from it, being in the utmost need of it, for their drinking, their crops, and their fruits, as He, exalted is He, said: {And He is the One who sends down the rain after they had despaired, and spreads His mercy, and He is the Protector, the Praiseworthy} [al-Shura: 28]. And He, exalted is He, said: {So look at the effects of the mercy of Allah, how He gives life to the earth after its death. Indeed, that is the One who gives life to the dead, and He is over all things capable} [al-Rum: 50].

His saying: {And We have certainly distributed it among them that they may remember}, meaning: We made it rain on this land and not on that, and We drove the clouds so that they passed over one land, going beyond it and crossing over it to another land, [so it rained on that one and gave it its fill, making it a fruitful land, while the land beyond it] did not have a single drop of water fall upon it. And in that He has the decisive proof and the conclusive wisdom.

Ibn Mas'ud and Ibn 'Abbas said: No year has more rain than another, but Allah distributes it as He wills. Then he recited this verse: {And We have certainly distributed it among them that they may remember, but most of mankind refuse except to disbelieve}.

Meaning: that they may remember, through Allah's giving life to the dead earth, that He is capable of giving life to the dead and to decayed bones. Or: that whoever is deprived of rain may remember that what befell him was because of a sin he committed, so that he may desist from what he is engaged in.

'Umar, the freedman of Ghufrah, said: Gabriel, peace be upon him, was in the place of funerals, and the Prophet ﷺ said to him: "O Gabriel, I would like to know the matter of the clouds." Gabriel said: "O Prophet of Allah, this is the angel in charge of the clouds, so ask him." He said: There come to us sealed decrees: "Water such and such lands, such and such an amount of rain." Reported by Ibn Hatim, and it is a mursal (report with a missing link to the Prophet) hadith.

His saying: {But most of mankind refuse except to disbelieve}: 'Ikrimah said: meaning those who say, "We were given rain by such and such a star (naw')."

What 'Ikrimah said is confirmed by what is authentically established in the hadith recorded in Sahih Muslim, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said to his companions one day, following a rainfall that had come upon them during the night: "Do you know what your Lord has said?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "He said: This morning, among My servants there is a believer in Me and a disbeliever. As for the one who said, 'We were given rain by the bounty and mercy of Allah,' that one is a believer in Me and a disbeliever in the star. And as for the one who said, 'We were given rain by such and such a naw',' that one is a disbeliever in Me and a believer in the star."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

وَهَذَا أَيْضًا مِنْ قُدْرَتِهِ التَّامَّةِ وَسُلْطَانِهِ الْعَظِيمِ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى يُرْسِلُ الرِّيَاحَ مُبَشِّرَاتٍ، أَيْ: بِمَجِيءِ السَّحَابِ بَعْدَهَا، وَالرِّيَاحُ أَنْوَاعٌ، فِي صِفَاتٍ كَثِيرَةٍ مِنَ التَّسْخِيرِ، فَمِنْهَا مَا يُثِيرُ السَّحَابَ، وَمِنْهَا مَا يَحْمِلُهُ، وَمِنْهَا مَا يَسُوقُهُ، وَمِنْهَا مَا يَكُونُ بَيْنَ يَدَيِ السَّحَابِ مبشِّرا، وَمِنْهَا مَا يَكُونُ قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ يَقُمّ الْأَرْضَ، وَمِنْهَا مَا يَلْقَحُ السَّحَابَ لِيُمْطِرَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَنزلْنَا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً طَهُورًا﴾ أَيْ: آلَةً يُتَطَهَّرُ بِهَا، كالسَّحُور وَالْوَقُودِ وَمَا جَرَى مَجْرَاهُ. فَهَذَا أَصَحُّ مَا يُقَالُ فِي ذَلِكَ. وَأَمَّا مَنْ قَالَ: إِنَّهُ فَعُولٌ بِمَعْنَى فَاعِلٍ، أَوْ: إِنَّهُ مَبْنِيٌّ لِلْمُبَالَغَةِ أَوِ التَّعَدِّي، فَعَلَى كُلٍّ مِنْهُمَا إِشْكَالَاتٌ مِنْ حَيْثُ اللُّغَةُ وَالْحُكْمُ، لَيْسَ هَذَا مَوْضِعَ بَسْطِهَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ حَفْصِ بْنِ غِيَاثٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، عَنْ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيِّ، حَدَّثَنِي حُمَيد الطَّوِيلُ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ الْبُنَانِيِّ قَالَ: دَخَلْتُ مَعَ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ فِي يَوْمٍ مَطِيرٍ، وَطُرُقُ الْبَصْرَةِ قَذِرَةٌ، فَصَلَّى، فَقُلْتُ لَهُ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَأَنزلْنَا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً طَهُورًا﴾ قَالَ: طَهَّرَهُ مَاءُ السَّمَاءِ.

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَلَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا وُهَيب عَنْ دَاوُدَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَأَنزلْنَا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً طَهُورًا﴾ [قَالَ: أَنْزَلَهُ اللَّهُ مَاءً طَاهِرًا] لَا يُنَجِّسُهُ شَيْءٌ.

وَعَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قِيلَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَنَتَوَضَّأُ مِنْ بِئْرِ بُضَاعَةَ؟ -وَهِيَ بِئْرٌ يُلقَى فِيهَا النَّتَن، وَلُحُومُ الْكِلَابِ -فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ الْمَاءَ طَهُورٌ لَا يُنَجِّسُهُ شَيْءٌ" رَوَاهُ الشَّافِعِيُّ، وَأَحْمَدُ وَصَحَّحَهُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ وَحَسَّنَهُ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْأَشْعَثِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعْتَمِرٌ، سَمِعْتُ أَبِي يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ سَيَّار، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، قَالَ: كَانَ عِنْدَ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ مَرْوَانَ، فَذَكَرُوا الْمَاءَ، فَقَالَ خَالِدُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ: مِنْهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، وَمِنْهُ مَا يَسْقِيهِ الْغَيْمُ مِنَ الْبَحْرِ فَيُعْذِبه الرَّعْدُ وَالْبَرْقُ. فَأَمَّا مَا كَانَ مِنَ الْبَحْرِ، فَلَا يَكُونُ لَهُ نَبَاتٌ، فَأَمَّا النَّبَاتُ فَمِمَّا كَانَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ.

وَرُوِيَ عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ قَالَ: مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ قَطْرَةً إِلَّا أَنْبَتَ بِهَا فِي الْأَرْضِ عُشْبَةً أَوْ فِي الْبَحْرِ لُؤْلُؤَةً. وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: فِي الْبَرِّ بُر، وَفِي الْبَحْرِ دُرّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِنُحْيِيَ بِهِ بَلْدَةً مَيْتًا﴾ أَيْ: أَرْضًا قَدْ طَالَ انْتِظَارُهَا لِلْغَيْثِ، فَهِيَ هَامِدَةٌ لَا نَبَاتَ فِيهَا وَلَا شَيْءَ. فَلَمَّا جَاءَهَا الْحَيَا عَاشَتْ وَاكْتَسَتْ رُبَاهَا أَنْوَاعُ الْأَزَاهِيرِ وَالْأَلْوَانِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَإِذَا أَنزلْنَا عَلَيْهَا الْمَاءَ اهْتَزَّتْ وَرَبَتْ وَأَنْبَتَتْ مِنْ كُلِّ زَوْجٍ بَهِيجٍ﴾ [الْحَجِّ: ٥] .

﴿وَنُسْقِيَهُ مِمَّا خَلَقْنَا أَنْعَامًا وَأَنَاسِيَّ كَثِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلِيَشْرَبَ مِنْهُ الْحَيَوَانُ مِنْ أَنْعَامٍ وَأَنَاسِيِّ مُحْتَاجِينَ إِلَيْهِ غَايَةَ الْحَاجَةِ، لِشُرْبِهِمْ وَزُرُوعِهِمْ وَثِمَارِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي يُنزلُ الْغَيْثَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا قَنَطُوا وَيَنْشُرُ رَحْمَتَهُ وَهُوَ الْوَلِيُّ الْحَمِيدُ﴾ [الشُّورَى: ٢٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَانْظُرْ إِلَى آثَارِ رَحْمَةِ اللَّهِ كَيْفَ يُحْيِي الأرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا إِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَمُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٥٠] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ صَرَّفْنَاهُ بَيْنَهُمْ لِيَذَّكَّرُوا﴾ أَيْ: أَمْطَرْنَا هَذِهِ الْأَرْضَ دُونَ هَذِهِ، وَسُقْنَا السَّحَابَ فَمَرَّ عَلَى الْأَرْضِ وَتَعَدَّاهَا وَجَاوَزَهَا إلى الأرض الأخرى، [فأمطرتها وكفتها فجعلتها عذقا، وَالَّتِي وَرَاءَهَا] لَمْ يَنْزِلْ فِيهَا قَطْرَةٌ مِنْ مَاءٍ، وَلَهُ فِي ذَلِكَ الْحُجَّةُ الْبَالِغَةُ وَالْحِكْمَةُ القاطعة.

قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ وَابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: لَيْسَ عَامٌ بِأَكْثَرَ مَطَرًا مِنْ عَامٍ، وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ يُصَرِّفُهُ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ صَرَّفْنَاهُ بَيْنَهُمْ لِيَذَّكَّرُوا فَأَبَى أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ إِلا كُفُورًا﴾ .

أَيْ: لِيَذَّكَّرُوا بِإِحْيَاءِ اللَّهِ الْأَرْضَ الْمَيِّتَةَ أَنَّهُ قَادِرٌ عَلَى إِحْيَاءِ الْأَمْوَاتِ . وَالْعِظَامِ الرُّفَاتِ. أَوْ: لِيَذَّكَّرَ مِنْ مَنْعِ القَطْر أَنَّمَا أَصَابَهُ ذَلِكَ بِذَنْبٍ أَصَابَهُ، فَيُقْلِعُ عَمَّا هُوَ فِيهِ.

وَقَالَ عُمَر مَوْلَى غُفْرَة : كَانَ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي مَوْضِعِ الْجَنَائِزِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "يَا جِبْرِيلُ، إِنِّي أُحِبُّ أَنْ أَعْلَمَ أمْرَ السَّحَابِ؟ " قَالَ: فَقَالَ جِبْرِيلُ: يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ، هَذَا مَلِكُ السَّحَابِ فَسَلْهُ. فَقَالَ: تَأْتِينَا صَكاك مُخَتَّمة: اسْقِ بِلَادَ كَذَا وَكَذَا، كَذَا وَكَذَا قَطْرَةً. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ حَاتِمٍ، وَهُوَ حَدِيثٌ مُرْسَلٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَبَى أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ إِلا كُفُورًا﴾ : قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: يَعْنِي: الَّذِينَ يَقُولُونَ: مُطِرْنَا بنَوء كَذَا وَكَذَا.

وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ عِكْرِمَةُ كَمَا صَحَّ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الْمُخْرَجِ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ لِأَصْحَابِهِ يوماً، عَلَى أَثَرِ سَمَاءٍ أَصَابَتْهُمْ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ: "أَتَدْرُونَ مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ" قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "قَالَ: أَصْبَحَ مِنْ عِبَادِي مُؤْمِنٌ بِي وَكَافِرٌ، فَأَمَّا مَنْ قَالَ: مُطِرْنَا بِفَضْلِ اللَّهِ وَرَحْمَتِهِ فَذَاكَ مُؤْمِنٌ بِي كَافِرٌ بِالْكَوْكَبِ. وَأَمَّا مَنْ قَالَ: مُطِرْنَا بِنَوْءِ كَذَا وَكَذَا، فَذَاكَ كَافِرٌ بِي، مُؤْمِنٌ بِالْكَوْكَبِ" .

---

## 25:51-54 — verses 51-54 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {Had We willed, We could have sent into every town a warner} calling them to Allah, Mighty and Majestic is He. But We singled you out, O Muhammad, for the mission to all the people of the earth, and We commanded you to convey this Qur'an to the people, {that I may warn you thereby, and whomever it reaches} [al-An'am: 19], {and whoever disbelieves in it among the factions, the Fire is his appointed place} [Hud: 17], {and that you may warn the mother of towns and those around it} [al-An'am: 92], {Say: O mankind, indeed I am the Messenger of Allah to you all} [al-A'raf: 158]. And in the two Sahihs: "I was sent to the red and the black," and in them both: "The prophet used to be sent to his people specifically, while I have been sent to mankind generally." For this reason He said: {So do not obey the disbelievers, and strive against them by means of it}, meaning by the Qur'an, as Ibn Abbas said, {a great striving}, just as the Almighty said: {O Prophet, strive against the disbelievers and the hypocrites and be harsh with them} [al-Tawbah: 73, al-Tahrim: 9].

Concerning His saying: {And He is the One who released the two seas, this one sweet and fresh, and this one salty and bitter}, meaning: He created the two waters, the sweet and the salty. The sweet is like rivers, springs, and wells, and this is the sweet sea, fresh and pure, al-furat. This was said by Ibn Jurayj, and Ibn Jarir chose it, and this is a matter beyond doubt, for there does not exist in the world a still sea that is sweet and fresh. Allah, glory be to Him, only informs of what actually is, so as to alert His servants to His favors upon them, that they might give thanks to Him. The sweet sea is this one that flows freely among people; the Almighty distributed it among His creation, because of their need for it, as rivers and springs in every land, according to their need and sufficiency for themselves and their lands.

Concerning His saying: {and this one salty and bitter}, meaning: salty, bitter, briny, unpalatable. This is like the well known seas in the east and west: the encompassing ocean and what connects to it of straits, the Sea of al-Qulzum, the Sea of Yemen, the Sea of Basra, the Sea of Persia, the Sea of China and India, the Sea of Rome, and the Sea of Khazar, and whatever resembles and is similar to them among the still seas that do not flow but rather wave, churn, and rage in wintertime and under strong winds. Among them are those that have tides, ebb and flow: at the beginning of each month a rise and flood occurs in them, and when the month begins to wane they recede, until they return to their original starting point. Then when the crescent of the next month appears they begin to rise again until the fourteenth night, then they begin to recede. Allah, glory be to Him and Exalted is He, to whom belongs complete power, made this into a recurring pattern. All these still seas, Allah, glory be to Him and Exalted is He, created with salty water, so that no foul stench of air would arise from them and thereby corrupt existence, and so that the land would not be poisoned by what dies in them of creatures. Since their water is salty, their air remains wholesome and their dead creatures are pure. For this reason the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, when asked about seawater, "Shall we perform wudu with it?" said: "It is pure, its water is purifying, and its dead [creatures] are lawful." Narrated by the imams: Malik, al-Shafi'i, Ahmad, and the compilers of the Sunan, with a sound chain.

Concerning His saying: {and He placed between them a barrier and a forbidding partition}, meaning: between the sweet and the salty, {a barzakh (barrier)}, meaning: a separator, which is dry land, {and a forbidding partition}, meaning: something preventing either of them from reaching the other, just as He said: {He released the two seas, meeting together, between them is a barzakh (barrier) which they do not transgress. So which of the favors of your Lord will you both deny?} [al-Rahman: 19-21]. And the Almighty said: {Or who has made the earth a stable resting place and placed within it rivers and made for it firmly set mountains and placed between the two seas a barrier? Is there a god with Allah? Rather, most of them do not know} [al-Naml: 61].

Concerning His saying: {And He is the One who created from water a human being, and made him one of lineage and one of marriage relation, and your Lord is ever Capable}, meaning: He created man from a weak drop of fluid, then fashioned him and made him proportionate, giving him a complete form, male or female, as He wills. {and made him one of lineage and one of marriage relation}: at the start of his existence he is a child related by lineage, then he marries and becomes one related by marriage, then he acquires in-laws and relatives by marriage and kinship. And all of this comes from a despised fluid. For this reason He said: {and your Lord is ever Capable}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ شِئْنَا لَبَعَثْنَا فِي كُلِّ قَرْيَةٍ نَذِيرًا﴾ يَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَلَكِنَّا خَصَصْنَاكَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -بِالْبِعْثَةِ إِلَى جَمِيعِ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ، وَأَمَرْنَاكَ أَنَّ تُبَلِّغَ النَّاسَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ، ﴿لأنْذِرَكُمْ بِهِ وَمَنْ بَلَغَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٩] ، ﴿وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِهِ مِنَ الأحْزَابِ فَالنَّارُ مَوْعِدُهُ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٧] ﴿وَلِتُنْذِرَ أُمَّ الْقُرَى وَمَنْ حَوْلَهَا﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٩٢] ، ﴿قُلْ يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنِّي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْكُمْ جَمِيعًا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٨] . وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "بُعِثْتُ إِلَى الْأَحْمَرِ وَالْأَسْوَدِ" وَفِيهِمَا: "وَكَانَ النَّبِيُّ يُبْعَثُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ خَاصَّةً وَبُعِثْتُ إِلَى النَّاسِ عَامَّةً"؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَلا تُطِعِ الْكَافِرِينَ وَجَاهِدْهُمْ بِهِ﴾ يَعْنِي: بِالْقُرْآنِ، قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ ﴿جِهَادًا كَبِيرًا﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ جَاهِدِ الْكُفَّارَ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ وَاغْلُظْ عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ٧٣،التَّحْرِيمِ: ٩] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي مَرَجَ الْبَحْرَيْنِ هَذَا عَذْبٌ فُرَاتٌ وَهَذَا مِلْحٌ أُجَاجٌ﴾ أَيْ: خَلَقَ الْمَاءَيْنِ: الْحُلْوَ وَالْمِلْحَ، فَالْحُلْوُ كَالْأَنْهَارِ وَالْعُيُونِ وَالْآبَارِ، وَهَذَا هُوَ الْبَحْرُ الْحُلْوُ الْفُرَاتُ الْعَذْبُ الزُّلَالُ. قَالَهُ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَهَذَا الَّذِي لَا شَكَّ فِيهِ، فَإِنَّهُ لَيْسَ فِي الْوُجُودِ بَحْرٌ سَاكِنٌ وَهُوَ عَذْبٌ فُرَاتٌ. وَاللَّهُ سُبْحَانَهُ إِنَّمَا أَخْبَرَ بِالْوَاقِعِ لِيُنَبِّهَ الْعِبَادَ عَلَى نِعَمِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ لِيَشْكُرُوهُ، فَالْبَحْرُ الْعَذْبُ هُوَ هَذَا السَّارِحُ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ، فَرَقَهُ تَعَالَى بَيْنَ خِلْقِهِ لِاحْتِيَاجِهِمْ إِلَيْهِ أَنْهَارًا وَعُيُونًا فِي كُلِّ أَرْضٍ بِحَسَبِ حَاجَتِهِمْ وَكِفَايَتِهِمْ لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ وَأَرَاضِيهِمْ.

* *
